***фамилия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фамилия.html>фами́лия</a> (761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Familie</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">familia</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">familia</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамилия.html>фами́лия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">famílija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамилия.html>фами́лии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамилия.html>фами́лии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамилия.html>фами́лий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>surname, last name, family name</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clan</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> family (<i>the original meaning</i>), see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамильный.html>фами́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">famílʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамильярный.html>фамилья́рный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">familʹjárnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамильярность.html>фамилья́рность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">familʹjárnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамильярность.html>фамилья́рности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамильярность.html>фамилья́рности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамильярность.html>фамилья́рностей</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фамильярный.html>фамилья́рный</a> (24186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">familiarny</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">familiāris</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фамильярный.html>фамилья́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">familʹjárnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)фамилья́рнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)фамилья́рней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>familiar, unceremonious <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">inappropriately intimate or friendly</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фанат.html>фана́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fanát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фанат.html>фана́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фанат.html>фана́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фанат.html>фана́тов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">фана́тка</b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фанера.html>фане́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fanéra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фанера.html>фане́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фанера.html>фане́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фанера.html>фане́р</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фанерный.html>фане́рный</a></b>)

<ol><li>to fantasize, to dream <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to indulge in fantasy</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фантазия.html>фанта́зия</a> (3553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантазия.html>фанта́зия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fantázija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантазия.html>фанта́зии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантазия.html>фанта́зии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантазия.html>фанта́зий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fantasy <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">imagining</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>фан<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:зи.html>зи</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фантасмагория.html>фантасмаго́рия</a> (31840)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантасмагория.html>фантасмаго́рия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fantasmagórija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантасмагория.html>фантасмаго́рии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантасмагория.html>фантасмаго́рии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантасмагория.html>фантасмаго́рий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>phantasmagoria (a dreamlike state)</li>
<li>nonsense, ridiculousness, absurdity</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фантаст.html>фанта́ст</a> (13439)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fantast</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантаст.html>фанта́ст</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fantást</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантаст.html>фанта́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантаст.html>фанта́сты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантаст.html>фанта́стов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dreamer, fantasist</li>
<li>visionary</li>
<li>science fiction writer</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фантик.html>фа́нтик</a> (29937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фант.html>фант</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fant</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантик.html>фа́нтик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fántik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантик.html>фа́нтика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>фа́нтики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фантик.html>фа́нтиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фант.html>фант</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fant</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (small) fant <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">object whose owner must perform a comic task in the game of fant, or the task so performed</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>candy wrapper
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>Мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сын</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:коллекционировать.html>коллекциони́рует</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>фа́нтики</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Moj syn kollekcionírujet <b>fántiki</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My son collects <b>candy wrappers</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фа.html>фа́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-фар-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фа.html>фа</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>о́н</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:карточный.html>ка́рточная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:фараон.html>фарао́н</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:фараон.html>фарао́ны</a></i>).

***фарт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фарт.html>фарт</a> (29324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фарт.html>фарт</a></b>  |  Russian fenya cant <i><a href = vnd.unilang:фарт.html>фарт</a></i>  |  <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">possibly</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> German Fahrt (ride)  |  German fahren (to drive, <a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a>) because <a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a> means both <i>to drive</i> and <i>to have luck</i> in Russian; or <i>possibly</i> from <a href = vnd.unilang:фортуна.html>форту́на</a> (fortune) meaning luck.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фарт.html>фарт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fart</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фарт.html>фа́рта</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">singular only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> luck, fortune</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> destiny</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***фартук.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фартук.html>фа́ртук</a> (9295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">fartuch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">vortuoch</i> (regional <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Vortuch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">apron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Compare dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">фа́ртух</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fártux</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">фарту́х</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fartúx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">хварту́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvartúk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фартук.html>фа́ртук</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fártuk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фартук.html>фа́ртука</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фартук.html>фа́ртуки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фартук.html>фа́ртуков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>apron (clothing)</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">فغفوری</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fağfûrî</span>, <span </p>
<ol><li><i>(a command to a dog)</i> attack!, get'em!, bite!</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">phaseolus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фасоль.html>фасо́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fasólʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фасоль.html>фасо́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фасоль.html>фасо́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фасоль.html>фасо́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>common bean, string bean</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фат.html>фат</a> (27078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fat</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fatus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stupid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фат.html>фат</a></b>
